**File:** `ai_admin/server.py`
**Line:** 136
**Context:** except
**Content:** `except Exception as e:
    logger = get_logger('ai_admin')
    logger.error(f'Server startup failed: {e}')
    if 'SSL' in str(e) or 'certificate' in str(e).lower():
        logger.error('SSL/Certificate related error detected')
        logger.error('Please check your SSL configuration and certificate files')
    elif 'mTLS' in str(e) or 'mutual' in str(e).lower():
        logger.error('mTLS related error detected')
        logger.error('Please check your mTLS configuration and client certificates')
    elif 'token' in str(e).lower():
        logger.error('Token authentication related error detected')
        logger.error('Please check your token configuration and JWT settings')
    sys.exit(1)`
